Wrangling the Beatles song writing using Python in FME(Safe Software)

Published: Sat 01 January 2022
By Alex

In python.

In [5]:
import requests
from bs4 import BeautifulSoup

# Make a request to the Wikipedia page
response = requests.get('https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/List_of_songs_recorded_by_the_Beatles')

# Parse the HTML content
soup = BeautifulSoup(response.text, 'html.parser')

# Find the data you want to scrape
title = soup.find('h1', class_='firstHeading').text

tr_elements = soup.find_all('tr')

# Iterate over the tr elements

content = soup.find('div', class_='mw-parser-output').text

# Extract the data
print(title)
print(content)

Take a look at the input¶

I will use Python Caller to manipulate attributes in FME and as input I want to take data that make sense to me: the Beatles!

Below you se my input that I pulled from here: https://ultimateclassicrock.com/who-wrote-the-most-beatles-songs/


| Song title                     | George Harrison  | John Lennon  | Paul McCartney  | Ringo Starr  |
|--------------------------------|------------------|--------------|-----------------|--------------|
| "Please Please Me"             |                  | 0            |                 |              |
| "Love Me Do"                   |                  |              | 0               |              |
| "Strawberry Fields Forever"    |                  | 0            |                 |              |
| "Octopus' Garden"              | 0                |              |                 | 1            |
| "Don't Pass Me By"             |                  |              |                 | 0            |
| "While My Guitar Gently Weeps" | 0                |              |                 |              |
| "I Want to Hold Your Hand      |                  | 0            | 1               |              |

First I use PythonCreator to instantiate FME objects that I then will be able to manipulate:

attr_names = ['Song title', 'George Harrison', 'John Lennon', 'Paul McCartney', 'Ringo Starr']
data_raw = '''"Please Please Me", None, 0, None, None
"Love Me Do", None, None, 0,None
"Strawberry Fields Forever", None, 0, None, None
"Octopus' Garden", 0,None, None, 1
"Don't Pass Me By", None, None, None, 0
"While My Guitar Gently Weeps", 0, None, None, None
"I Want to Hold Your Hand, None, 0,1, None'''

data_clean = [[ii 
          for ii in i.split(',')
          ] 
          for i in data_raw.split('\n')]
where_beatles = r'C:\thisAKcode.github.io\Pelican\content\other\beatles_auth.csv'
